<P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-
family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><A NAME="tx576647_9"></A>NOTES TO 
CONSOLIDATED FINANCIAL STATEMENTS </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-
family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>(UNAUDITED) </B></FONT></P> <P 
STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>N<SMALL>OTE</SMALL> 
1&#151;S<SMALL>UMMARY</SMALL> <SMALL>OF</SMALL> <SMALL>SIGNIFICANT</SMALL> 
<SMALL>ACCOUNTING</SMALL> <SMALL>POLICIES</SMALL> </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" 
ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">CGG 
(&#147;the Company&#148;) and its subsidiaries (together, the &#147;Group&#148;)
is a global participant in the
geophysical and geological services industry, providing a wide range of data 
acquisition, processing and interpretation services as well as related imaging 
and interpretation software to clients in the oil and gas exploration and 
production
business. It is also a global manufacturer of geophysical equipment. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" 
ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Given that 
the Company is listed on a
European Stock Exchange and pursuant to European regulation n&deg;1606/2002 
dated July&nbsp;19, 2002, the accompanying interim condensed consolidated 
financial statements have been prepared in accordance with IAS34 as issued by 
the International
Accounting Standards Board (IASB) and adopted by the European Union. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" 
ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">These interim
condensed consolidated
financial statements have been authorized by the Board of Directors for issue on
July&nbsp;31, 2013. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; 
text-indent:4%" ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" 
SIZE="2">The
preparation of consolidated financial statements in accordance with IFRS 
requires management to make estimates, assumptions and judgments that affect the
reported amounts of assets and liabilities and disclosure of contingent assets 
and liabilities
at the date of the consolidated financial statements and the reported amounts of
revenues and expenses during the reporting period. Actual results could differ 
materially from those estimates due to the change in economic conditions, 
changes in laws
and regulations, changes in strategy and the inherent imprecision associated 
with the use of estimates. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-
bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New 
Roman" SIZE="2">The
interim condensed consolidated financial statements are presented in U.S. dollar
and have been prepared on a historical cost basis, except for certain financial 
assets and liabilities that have been measured at fair value. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New 
Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Critical accounting policies </B></FONT></P> <P 
STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" ALIGN="justify"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The interim condensed consolidated 
financial statements do not include all the information and disclosures required
in the annual financial statements, and should be read in conjunction with the
Group&#146;s annual financial statements as of and for the year ended 
December&nbsp;31, 2012 included in its report on Form 20-F for the year 2012 
filed with the SEC on April&nbsp;25, 2013. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" 
ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The 
accounting policies adopted in the preparation of the interim condensed
consolidated financial statements are
consistent with those followed in the preparation of the Group&#146;s annual 
financial statements for the year ended December&nbsp;31, 2012, except for the 
adoption of the following new Standards and Interpretations: </FONT></P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-
family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">
statements. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT 
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><I>Change in accounting policies
</I></B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" 
ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Starting 
January&nbsp;1, 2013, we have applied IAS19 revised &#150; Employee benefits. As
the application of this new
standard is a change of accounting policy, all comparative financial information
has been restated to present comparative amounts for each period presented as if
the new accounting policy had always been applied. As a result: </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" 
CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New 
Roman" SIZE="2">&#149;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times
New Roman" SIZE="2">As the Group already recognizes actuarial gains and losses 
in other comprehensive income (OCI), this specific amendment had no impact on 
the
consolidated financial statements. </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-
size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" 
CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New 
Roman" SIZE="2">&#149;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times
New Roman" SIZE="2">Unvested past services costs are no longer recognized as an 
expense on a straight-line basis over the average period until the benefits 
become
vested, but are recognized immediately if the benefits have vested immediately 
following the introduction of, or changes to, a pension plan. 
</FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-
bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" 
CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times
New Roman" SIZE="2">Discounting effect is now calculated on the amount of the 
net defined benefit liability. Interests in the profit and loss are now 
calculated using
the discount rate used to measure the defined benefit obligation. 
</FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-
indent:4%" ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" 
SIZE="2">The adjustments resulting
from the immediate recognition of past services costs are as follows:

</TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-
family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><I>Change in estimate </I></B></FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" ALIGN="justify"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The useful life of our 
&#147;Sentinel&#148; solid streamers was reassessed from 7 to 6 years. 
Accordingly, starting January&nbsp;1, 2013, we calculated depreciation expenses 
over the revised useful life
for the remaining periods. This change has been applied prospectively and does 
not affect previous years. The effect of this change for the six months ended 
June&nbsp;30, 2013 is as follows: </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0"

<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times
New Roman" SIZE="2">Increase in depreciation expenses in operating income of 
U.S.$6.6 million, </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" 
CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New 
Roman" SIZE="2">&#149;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times
New Roman" SIZE="2">Decrease in the carrying amount of property, plant and 
equipment of U.S.$6.6 million </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New 
Roman" SIZE="2"><B><I>Operating revenues </I></B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-
top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" ALIGN="justify"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Operating revenues are recognized 
when they can be measured reliably, and when it is likely that the economic 
benefits associated with the transaction will flow to the entity, which is at 
the point that
such revenues have been realized or are considered realizable. </FONT></P> <P 
STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" 
CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New 
Roman" SIZE="2">&#149;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times
New Roman" SIZE="2"><I>Multi-client surveys</I> </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P
STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" ALIGN="justify"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Revenues related to multi-client 
surveys result from (i)&nbsp;pre-commitments and (ii)&nbsp;licenses after 
completion of the surveys (&#147;after-sales&#148;). </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" 
ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><I>Pre-
commitments</I>&nbsp;&#150; Generally, we obtain commitments from a limited 
number of customers before a
seismic/geological project is completed. These pre-commitments cover part or all
of the survey area blocks. In return for the commitment, the customer typically 
gains the right to direct or influence the project specifications, advance 
access to
data as it is being acquired, and favorable pricing. We record payments that we 
receive during periods of mobilization as advance billing on the balance sheet 
in the line item &#147;Advance billings to customers&#148;. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" 
ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Once 
production has started, we recognize pre-commitments as revenue as services are 
rendered, based on the physical
progress of the project. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-
bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New 
Roman" SIZE="2"><I>After sales</I>&nbsp;&#150; Generally, we grant a license 
entitling non-exclusive
access to a complete and ready-for-use, specifically defined portion of our 
multi-client data library in exchange for a fixed and determinable payment. We 
recognize after sales revenue upon the client executing a valid license 
agreement and having
been granted access to the data. We provide a warranty that the medium on which 
the data is transmitted (a magnetic cartridge) is free from technical defects, 
which the client may exercise during the thirty days from execution and access. 
If the
warranty is exercised, the Company will provide the same data on a new magnetic 
cartridge. The cost of providing new magnetic cartridges is negligible. 
</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">In case after sales agreements 
contain multiple deliverable elements, the revenue is allocated to the various 
elements based on specific objective evidence of fair value, regardless of any 
separate
allocations stated within the contract for each element. Each element is 
appropriately accounted for under the applicable accounting standard. 
</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" 
ALIGN="justify"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><I>After sales volume 
agreements</I>&nbsp;&#150; We enter into a customer arrangement in which we 
agree to grant licenses to the customer for access to a specified number of 
blocks of the multi-client
library. These arrangements typically enable the customer to select and access 
the specific blocks for a limited period of time. We recognize revenue when the 
blocks are selected and the client has been granted access to the data, if the
corresponding revenue can be reliably estimated. We provide a warranty that the 
medium on which the data is transmitted (a magnetic cartridge) is free from 
technical defects, which the client may exercise during the thirty days from 
execution and
access. If the warranty is exercised, the Company will provide the same data on 
a new magnetic cartridge. The cost of providing new magnetic cartridges is 
negligible. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-
bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" 
CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New
Roman" SIZE="2">&#149;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times
New Roman" SIZE="2"><I>Exclusive surveys</I> </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P 
STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" ALIGN="justify"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">In exclusive surveys, we perform 
seismic services (acquisition and processing) for a specific customer. We 
recognize proprietary/contract revenues as the services are rendered. We 
evaluate the progress to
date, in a manner generally consistent with the physical progress of the 
project, and we recognize revenues based on the ratio of the project cost 
incurred during that period to the total estimated project costs as far as they 
can reliably be
assessed. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-
indent:4%" ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" 
SIZE="2">The billings and the costs related to the transit of seismic vessels at
the beginning of the survey
are deferred and recognized over the duration of the contract by reference to 
the technical stage of completion. </FONT></P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-
family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">- 12 -
</FONT></P>
<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
<h5 align="left"><a href="#toc">Table of Contents</a></h5>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" 
ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">In some 
exclusive survey contracts and a limited number of multi-client
survey contracts, we are required to meet certain milestones. We defer 
recognition of revenue on such contracts until all milestones that provide the 
customer a right of cancellation or refund of amounts paid have been met. 
</FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" 
CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New 
Roman" SIZE="2">&#149;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times
New Roman" SIZE="2"><I>Equipment sales</I> </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P 
STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" ALIGN="justify"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">We recognize revenues on equipment 
sales upon delivery to the customer when risks and rewards are fully 
transferred. Any advance billings to customers are recorded in current 
liabilities. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" 
CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New 
Roman" SIZE="2">&#149;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times
New Roman" SIZE="2"><I>Software and hardware sales</I> 
</FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-
indent:4%" ALIGN="justify"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">We recognize revenues from the sale
of software and hardware products following acceptance of the product by the 
customer at which time we have no further significant vendor obligations 
remaining. Any
advance billings to customers are recorded in current liabilities. </FONT></P> 
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" 
ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">If an 
arrangement to deliver software,
either alone or together with other products or services, requires significant 
production, modification, or customization of software, the entire arrangement 
is accounted for as a production-type contract, i.e. using the percentage of 
completion
method. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"
ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">If the 
software arrangement provides for multiple deliverables (e.g. upgrades or 
enhancements,
post-contract customer support such as maintenance, or services), the revenue is
allocated to the various elements based on specific objective evidence of fair 
value, regardless of any separate allocations stated within the contract for 
each
element. Each element is appropriately accounted for under the applicable 
accounting standard. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; 
text-indent:4%" ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" 
SIZE="2">Maintenance
revenues consist primarily of post contract customer support agreements and are 
recorded as advance billings to customers and recognized as revenue on a 
proportional performance basis over the contract period. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" 
CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New 
Roman" SIZE="2">&#149;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times
New Roman" SIZE="2"><I>Other geophysical/geological sales or services</I> 
</FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" 
ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Revenues from
our other geophysical/geological sales or services are recognized as the 
services are performed and, when
related to long-term contracts, using the proportional performance method of 
recognizing revenues. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-
bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" 
CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New 
Roman" SIZE="2">&#149;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times
New Roman" SIZE="2"><I>Customer loyalty programs</I> 
</FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-
indent:4%" ALIGN="justify"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">We may grant award credits to our 
main clients. These award credits are contractually based on cumulative services
provided during the calendar year and attributable to future services. 
</FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" 
ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">These credits
are considered as a separate component of the initial sale and measured at their
fair value by reference to
the contractual rates and the forecasted cumulative revenues for the calendar
year. These proceeds are recognized as revenue only when the obligation has been
fulfilled. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><I>Multi-client surveys 
</I></B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" 
ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Multi-client 
surveys consist
of seismic or geological surveys to be licensed to customers on a non-exclusive 
basis. All costs directly incurred in acquiring, processing and otherwise 
completing surveys are capitalized into the multi-client surveys (including 
transit costs when
applicable). The value of our multi-client library is stated on our balance 
sheet at the aggregate of those costs less accumulated amortization or at fair 
value if lower. We review the library for potential impairment at each balance 
sheet date at
the relevant level (independent surveys or groups of surveys). </FONT></P> <P 
STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" ALIGN="justify"><FONT 
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">We amortize the multi-client 
surveys over the
period during which the data is expected to be marketed using an amortization 
rate applied to recognized revenues. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-
top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" ALIGN="justify"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Multi-client surveys are classified
into a same category when they are located in the same area with the same 
estimated sales ratio, such estimates generally relying on the historical 
patterns.
</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" 
ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Depending on 
the category of the survey, we generally use amortization rates from 50% to 
83.3% corresponding
to the ratio of total estimated costs over total estimated sales, unless 
specific indications lead to apply a different rate. </FONT></P> <P 
STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" ALIGN="justify"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Starting from the data delivery 
date, a minimum straight-line depreciation scheme is applied over a five-year 
period for seismic surveys and a seven-year period for geological surveys, if 
total
accumulated depreciation from the applicable amortization rate is </FONT></P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-
family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">- 13 -
</FONT></P>

STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><I>Development costs 
</I></B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" 
ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Expenditures 
on research activities undertaken with the prospect of gaining new scientific or
technological knowledge and
understanding are recognized in the income statement as expenses as incurred and
are presented as &#147;Research and development expenses&nbsp;&#150; net&#148;. 
Expenditures on development activities, whereby research finding are applied to 
a plan
or design for the production of new or substantially improved products and 
processes, are capitalized if: </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-
top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0"

identified and reliably measured, </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE>

feasible, </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times

benefits, either because it is useful to us or through an existing market for 
the

STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" ALIGN="justify"><FONT 
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The expenditures capitalized 
include the cost
of materials, direct labor and an appropriate proportion of overhead. Other 
development expenditures are recognized in the income statement as expenses as 
incurred and are presented as &#147;Research and development 
expenses&nbsp;&#150; net&#148;.
</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" 
ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Capitalized 
development expenditures are stated at cost less accumulated amortization and 
impairment losses.
</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" 
ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">We amortize 
capitalized developments costs over five&nbsp;years. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" 
ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman"
SIZE="2">Research&nbsp;&amp; development expenses in our income statement 
represent the net cost of development costs that are not
capitalized, of research costs, offset by government grants acquired for 
research and development. </FONT></P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New

<SMALL>AND</SMALL> <SMALL>DIVESTITURES</SMALL>
</B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-
left:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><I>Acquisition of 
Fugro&#146;s Geoscience Division </I></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" 
ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">On January 
31, 2013, we completed the acquisition of Fugro&#146;s Geoscience Division, with
the exception of the airborne
activity and certain minor assets which will be contributed at a later date. We 
paid to Fugro an amount of &#128;703 million (U.S.$953 million) after deduction 
of U.S.$281 million due by Fugro to increase its shareholding in the Seabed 
joint venture
to 60%. In addition, Fugro extended to us a &#128;125 million vendor loan with a
5 year maturity and bearing an interest rate of 5.5% per annum, which is to be 
increased to &#128;225 million at the date of effective acquisition of the 
airborne
business. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-

STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><I>Sale of the Company&#146;s 
shareholding interest in Spectrum ASA </I></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-
top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" ALIGN="justify"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">On February&nbsp;20, 2013, we sold 
all of the remaining shares we held in Spectrum ASA at NOK 47.50&nbsp;per share.
We recognized a U.S.$19.8 million gain recorded in the line item &#147;Other 
revenues
(expenses) net&#148; in our consolidated statement of operations. </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-
family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><I>Creation of a ship management joint-venture 
with Louis
Dreyfus Armateurs Group (LDA) </I></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-
bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New 
Roman" SIZE="2">On April&nbsp;16, 2013, CGG and Louis Dreyfus Armateurs Group 
(LDA) created
a ship management joint-venture, GeofieLD Ship Managements Services SAS. Co-
owned 50% by CGG and 50% by Louis Dreyfus Armateurs Group, the new joint-venture
will provide maritime ship management services for CGG&#146;s high-capacity 3D 
seismic
vessels. The company has been accounted for under equity method in our financial
statements since this date. </FONT></P>

</TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" 
ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The average 
price of CGG shares was &#128;18.95 and &#128;20.55 for the six months period
ended June&nbsp;30, 2013 and 2012, respectively. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-
top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" 
SIZE="2"><B>N<SMALL>OTE</SMALL> 4&#151;F<SMALL>INANCIAL</SMALL> 
<SMALL>DEBT</SMALL> </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" 
ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Gross 
financial debt as of June&nbsp;30, 2013 was U.S.$2,529.1 million compared to 
U.S.$2,305.2 million as of
December&nbsp;31, 2012. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"
ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">In 
conjunction with the acquisition of the Geoscience Division, U.S.$ 
117&nbsp;million of the vendor
loan granted by Fugro was classified as current portion of the financial debt. 
</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-
family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>N<SMALL>OTE</SMALL> 
5&#151;R<SMALL>ECEIVABLES</SMALL>
</B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" 
ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">During 2013, 
the Group entered into several factoring agreements with various banks. As of 
June&nbsp;30,
2013, we had transferred U.S.$47.2 million compared to U.S.$68.2 million as of 
December&nbsp;31, 2012 of notes receivable as part of these agreements. The 
risks retained by the Group are mainly the risk of payment delay up to 30 days
and the risk of
commercial litigation. Both have been historically low with the transferred 
clients. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-
indent:4%" ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">As
a consequence, the
Group retained only non-significant amounts to the extent of its continuing 
involvement. Related costs recorded in operating income are not significant. 
</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>N<SMALL>OTE</SMALL> 
6&#151;A<SMALL>NALYSIS</SMALL> <SMALL>BY</SMALL> <SMALL>SEGMENT</SMALL> 
<SMALL>AND</SMALL> <SMALL>GEOGRAPHIC</SMALL> <SMALL>AREA</SMALL> </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" 
ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">We previously
reported our results on the basis of two reportable segments: Geophysical 
Services and Geophysical
Equipment. As a result of the acquisition of Fugro&#146;s Geoscience Division, 
we changed our organization, as well as the way management measures our 
performance. Since February&nbsp;1, 2013, we have been organized in three 
Divisions: </FONT></P>

STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" ALIGN="justify"><FONT 
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Financial information by segment is
reported in
accordance with our internal reporting system and provides internal segment 
information that is used by the chief operating decision maker to manage and 
measure the performance. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" 
ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">We also 
changed our main performance indicator from operating income to earnings before 
interest and tax
(&#147;EBIT&#148;). We define EBIT as operating income plus our share of income 
in companies accounted for under the equity method. EBIT is used by management 
as a performance indicator because it captures the contribution to our results 
of the
significant businesses that we </FONT></P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-

<P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-
family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">
manage through our joint-ventures. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-
bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New 
Roman" SIZE="2">Prior period segment
disclosure has been restated to reflect the new segments. </FONT></P> <P 
STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" ALIGN="justify"><FONT 
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Inter-company transactions between 
segments are
made at arm&#146;s length prices. They relate primarily to geophysical equipment
sales made by the Equipment segment to the Acquisition segment and to services 
rendered by the Acquisition segment to the GGR segment for the multi-client 
seismic
library. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-
indent:4%" ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" 
SIZE="2">These inter-segment revenues and the related earnings are eliminated in
consolidation in the tables
that follow under the column &#147;Eliminations and other&#148;. </FONT></P> <P 
STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" ALIGN="justify"><FONT 
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The inter-segment sales and the 
related
earnings recognized by the Equipment segment are eliminated and presented in the
tables that follow as follows: (i)&nbsp;EBIT for our Acquisition segment is 
presented after elimination of amortization expenses corresponding to capital 
expenditures
between our Equipment segment and Acquisition segment; and (ii)&nbsp;capital 
expenditures for our Acquisition segment are presented after elimination of 
inter-segment margin. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" 
ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">EBIT may 
include non-recurring items, which are disclosed in the reportable segment if 
material. General corporate
expenses, which include Group management, financing, and legal activities, have 
been included in the column &#147;Eliminations and other&#148; in the tables 
that follow. The Group does not disclose financial expenses or financial 
revenues by segment
because they are managed at the Group level. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-
top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-
family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Identifiable assets are those used in the 
operations of each
segment. Unallocated and corporate assets consist primarily of financial assets,
including cash and cash equivalents. Due to the constant changes in work 
locations, the group does not track its assets based on country of origin or 
ownership.
</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" 
ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Capital 
employed is defined as total assets excluding cash and cash equivalents less 
(i)&nbsp;current
liabilities excluding bank overdrafts and current portion of financial debt; and
(ii)&nbsp;non-current liabilities excluding financial debt. </FONT></P> <P 
STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" ALIGN="justify"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The following tables also present 
operating revenues and EBIT by reportable segment, and operating revenues by 
geographic area (by location of customers). </FONT></P>

<h5 align="left"><a href="#toc">Table of Contents</a></h5>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" 
ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Louis Dreyfus
Armateurs (&#147;LDA&#148;) provides ship management services
for a portion of our fleet. In addition, LDA is the owner, together with the 
Group, of Geomar which owns of the seismic vessel
&#147;<I>Aliz&eacute;</I>&#148;. Geomar provides vessel charter services to LDA.
</FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" 
ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Argas, 
Eidesvik Seismic Vessel AS, Oceanic Seismic Vessel AS, Gardline CGG Pte Ltd., 
CGG Eidesvik Ship Management, PTSC
CGGV Geophysical Survey Company, PT Elnusa-CGGVeritas Seismic, Geofield Ship 
Management Services and Seabed Geosolutions BV are accounted for under the 
equity method. Tronic&#146;s is 16% owned by the Group. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" 
ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">No credit 
facility or loan was granted to the Company by shareholders during the last 
three years. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New 
Roman" SIZE="2"><B>N<SMALL>OTE</SMALL> 9&#151;S<SMALL>UBSEQUENT</SMALL> 
<SMALL>EVENTS</SMALL> </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-
family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><I>Financing </I></B></FONT></P> <P 
STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" ALIGN="justify"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">On July&nbsp;1, 2013, CGG entered 
into a 5-year U.S.$200 million vessel financing, split into two tranches of U.S.
$100 million each, notably to reimburse the 2013 tranche of our vendor loan 
granted by
Fugro in connection with the acquisition of the Geoscience Division. We entered 
into an interest rate swap to fix the effective rate at 4.4%. </FONT></P> <P 
STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" ALIGN="justify"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">On July&nbsp;15, 2013, CGG entered 
into a new revolving credit facility of up to U.S.$165 million with a 5 years 
maturity. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" 
ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">On 
July&nbsp;22, 2013, CGG sent an early redemption notice for an amount of U.S.
$125 million of our Senior Notes due
2016. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" 
ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">On July 31, 
2013, CGG entered into a new French revolving facility of up to U.S.$325 million
with a 3
years maturity with two extension options of one year each. </FONT></P> <P 
STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-
family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><I>Litigation </I></B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" 
ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">In July 2013,
CGG do Brazil received a notice of reassessment covering the year 2009 for a 
total amount of U.S.$12
million. The tax authorities claim the withholding taxes and CIDE on charter 
payments. CGG do Brazil intends to appeal this reassessment. The Group does not 
expect this claim to have any material impact on the Group&#146;s financial 
statements.
</FONT></P>

STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" ALIGN="justify"><FONT 
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Financial information by segment is
reported in
accordance with our internal reporting system and provides internal segment 
information that is used by the chief operating decision maker to manage and 
measure the performance. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" 
ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">We also 
changed our main performance indicator from operating income to earnings before 
interest and tax
(&#147;EBIT&#148;). We define EBIT as operating income plus our share of income 
in companies accounted for under the equity method. EBIT is used by management 
as performance indicator because it captures the contribution to our results of 
the
significant businesses that we manage through our joint-ventures. </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" ALIGN="justify"><FONT 
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Prior period segment disclosure has
been
restated to reflect the new segments. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-
top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" 
SIZE="2"><B>Factors Affecting Results of Operations </B></FONT></P> <P 
STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><I>Geophysical market 
environment </I></B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; 
text-indent:4%" ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" 
SIZE="2">Overall demand for
geophysical services and equipment is dependent on spending by oil and gas 
companies for exploration, development and production and field management 
activities. We believe the level of spending of such companies depends on their 
assessment of their
ability to efficiently supply the oil and gas market in the future and the 
current balance of hydrocarbon supply and demand. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-
top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" ALIGN="justify"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The geophysical market has 
historically been extremely cyclical. We believe many factors contribute to the 
volatility of this market, such as the geopolitical uncertainties that can harm 
the confidence
and visibility that are essential to our clients&#146; long-term decision-making
processes and the expected balance in the mid to long term between supply and 
demand for hydrocarbons. Exploration&nbsp;&amp; Production companies have 
budgeted an
overall high single-digit increase in exploration and production spending with a
strong focus on international activity. This should continue to drive price 
increase in marine and overall volume growth in 2013. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" 
ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">See 
&#147;Item 4: Information on the Company &#150; Industry Conditions&#148; of our
annual report on Form 20-F for the
year ended December&nbsp;31, 2012 for a discussion of developments in the 
geophysical industry. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-
bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" 
SIZE="2"><B><I>Acquisitions and divestitures
</I></B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-
left:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><I>Acquisition of 
Fugro&#146;s Geoscience Division </I></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" 
ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">On 
January&nbsp;31, 2013, we completed the acquisition of Fugro&#146;s Geoscience 
Division, with the exception of the
airborne activity and certain minor assets which will be contributed at a later 
date. The purchase price amounted to U.S.$1,514 million leading to a preliminary
goodwill of U.S.$716 million. </FONT></P>

</TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" 
ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Our 
consolidated operating revenues for the three months ended June&nbsp;30, 2013
increased 24% to U.S.$1,032 million from U.S.$831 million for the comparable 
period of 2012, mainly as a result of the acquisition of Fugro&#146;s Geoscience
Division on January&nbsp;31, 2013, with a particularly strong impact in Marine 
due to the
integration of Fugro&#146;s fleet as of February&nbsp;1, 2013, and a high level 
of multi-client sales. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px; 
margin-left:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" 
SIZE="2"><U>Acquisition
</U></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" 
ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Operating 
revenues for our Acquisition segment, including intra-group sales, increased 30%
to U.S.$605
million for the three months ended June&nbsp;30, 2013 from U.S.$466 million for 
the comparable period of 2012, mainly due to strong operational performance by 
our Marine acquisition business line, with traditionally low activity in our 
Land
acquisition business in the second quarter. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-
top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-
family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Excluding intra-group sales, operating revenues
increased 19% to
U.S.$477 million for the three months ended June&nbsp;30, 2013 from U.S.$400 
million for the comparable period of 2012. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-
family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><I>Marine acquisition </I></FONT></P> <P 
STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" ALIGN="justify"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Operating revenues from our Marine 
acquisition business line for the three months ended June&nbsp;30, 2013 
increased 53% to U.S.$511 million from U.S.$335 million for the comparable 
period of 2012, mainly
due to the integration of Fugro&#146;s fleet as of February&nbsp;1, 2013. Marine
production was high for the whole fleet, with a record availability rate of 93% 
for the three months ended June&nbsp;30, 2013 compared to 91% for the three 
months ended
June&nbsp;30, 2012. The production rate also increased to 92% for the three 
months ended June&nbsp;30, 2013 from 91% for the three months ended 
June&nbsp;30, 2012. Almost half of the fleet was on Broadseis projects. The main
part of the fleet was
located in the North Sea (where six vessels were in operation), in the Gulf of 
Mexico (four vessels) and in Asia (six vessels). 21% of the fleet was dedicated 
to multi-client programs for the three months ended June&nbsp;30, 2013 compared 
to 17% for
the three months ended June&nbsp;30, 2012. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-
top:18px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New 
Roman" SIZE="2"><I>Land (and Airborne) acquisition </I></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" 
ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Operating 
revenues from our other acquisition businesses, including intra-group sales, 
decreased 28% to U.S.$94 million
for the three months ended June&nbsp;30, 2013, compared to U.S.$131 million for 
the three months ended June&nbsp;30, 2012. During this quarter, which is 
typically weaker, our land crews operated in difficult security and weather 
conditions. The
acquisition of Airborne is expected to be completed in early September 2013. 
</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%"><FONT 
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><U>Geology, Geophysics&nbsp;&amp; 
Reservoir
</U></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" 
ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Operating 
revenues from our GGR segment for the three months ended June&nbsp;30, 2013 
increased 84% to
U.S.$367 million from U.S.$200 million for the comparable period of 2012 due to 
a good performance across all businesses in a strong market. </FONT></P> <P 
STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><I>Multi-clients, basin data and 
Data Management </I></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; 
text-indent:4%" ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" 
SIZE="2">Multi-client
and basin data revenues increased significantly to U.S.$215 million for the 
three months ended June&nbsp;30, 2013 from U.S.$86 million for the three months 
ended June&nbsp;30, 2012. </FONT></P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-
family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">- 26 -
</FONT></P>
<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
<h5 align="left"><a href="#toc">Table of Contents</a></h5>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" 
ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Prefunding 
revenues were U.S.$87 million for the three months ended
June&nbsp;30, 2013 compared to U.S.$45 million for the three months ended 
June&nbsp;30, 2012, mainly focused in the Gulf of Mexico with the continuation 
of our IBALT program and onshore in Marcellus. The cash prefunding rate was 84% 
for the three
months ended June&nbsp;30, 2013 compared to 55% for the three months ended 
June&nbsp;30, 2012. After sales were at a high level across all regions and
particularly in Brazil, ahead of the October Santos pre-salt bid round. 
</FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-
family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><I>Imaging&nbsp;&amp; Reservoir </I></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" 
ALIGN="justify"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Operating revenues from our 
Imaging&nbsp;&amp; Reservoir business line increased 35% to U.S.$152 million for
the three months ended June&nbsp;30, 2013 from U.S.$114 million for the 
comparable period of
2012. The market for imaging and reservoir characterization businesses remains 
buoyant, sustained by an increasing volume of data in complex geologies. 
</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><I><U></U></I><U>Equipment<I> 
</I></U></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" 
ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Operating 
revenues for our
Equipment segment, including intra-group sales, decreased 11% to U.S.$254 
million for the three months ended June&nbsp;30, 2013 from U.S.$285&nbsp;million
for the comparable period of 2012. Sales were strong in Eastern Europe, Asia and
Russia. The
commercial success of UNITE, Sercel&#146;s wireless cable system has been 
confirmed by strong sales in North America and South America. Marine equipment 
sales represented 48% of total revenue. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-
family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Internal sales represented 26% of total revenue
for the three months ended June&nbsp;30, 2013. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" 
ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Excluding 
intra-group sales, operating revenues for our Equipment segment decreased 19% to
U.S.$188 million for the three
months ended June&nbsp;30, 2013 from U.S.$232 million for the comparable period 
of 2012. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT 
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><I>Operating Expenses 
</I></B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" 
ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Cost of 
operations, including depreciation and amortization, increased 21% to U.S.$794 
million for the three months ended
June&nbsp;30, 2013 from U.S.$654 million for the comparable period of 2012, 
mainly due to the integration of Fugro&#146;s Geoscience Division. The multi-
client amortization expenses correspond to 51% of multi-client revenues for the 
three months
ended June&nbsp;30, 2013 compared to 74% for the comparable period of 2012. As a
percentage of operating revenues, cost of operations decreased to 77% for the 
three months ended June&nbsp;30, 2013 from 79% for the comparable period of 
2012. Gross
profit increased 34% to U.S.$238 million for the three months ended 
June&nbsp;30, 2013 from U.S.$178 million for the comparable period of 2012, 
representing 23% and 21% of operating revenues, respectively. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" 
ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Research and 
development expenditures increased 10% to U.S.$25 million for the three months 
ended June&nbsp;30, 2013,
from U.S.$23 million for the comparable period of 2012, representing 2% and 3% 
of operating revenues, respectively. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-
top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" ALIGN="justify"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Marketing and selling expenses 
increased 40% to U.S.$35 million for the three months ended June&nbsp;30, 2013 
from U.S.$25 million for the comparable period of 2012. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" 
ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">General and 
administrative expenses increased 20% to U.S.$54 million for the three months 
ended June&nbsp;30, 2013 from
U.S.$45 million for the comparable period of 2012. As a percentage of operating 
revenues, general and administrative expenses represented 5% for both periods. 
</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><I>Equity in Income of 
Affiliates </I></B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-
indent:4%" ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" 
SIZE="2">Losses from
investments accounted for under the equity method amounted to U.S.$5 million for
the three months ended June&nbsp;30, 2013 compared to an income of U.S.$10 
million for the three months ended June&nbsp;30, 2012, mainly due to the slow 
start of our
Seabed joint venture with Fugro. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-
bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><I>Earnings 
before interest and tax (&#147;EBIT&#148;) </I></B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" 
ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">EBIT, as 
disclosed in note 6 to our Consolidated Financial Statements, increased to U.S.
$117 million for the three months
ended June&nbsp;30, 2013 from U.S.$96 million for the three months ended 
June&nbsp;30, 2012 as a result of the factors described above. </FONT></P> <P 
STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" ALIGN="justify"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">EBIT from our Acquisition segment 
increased to U.S.$28 million for the three months ended June&nbsp;30, 2013 from 
U.S.$5 million for the comparable period of 2012. EBIT margin was 5% for the 
three months
ended June&nbsp;30, 2013. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-
bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New 
Roman" SIZE="2">EBIT from our GGR segment increased to U.S.$96 million for the 
three months ended
June&nbsp;30, 2013 from U.S.$30 million for the comparable period of 2012. EBIT 
margin was 26% for the three months ended June&nbsp;30, 2013. </FONT></P> <P 
STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" ALIGN="justify"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">EBIT from our Equipment segment 
decreased to U.S.$71 million for three months ended June&nbsp;30, 2013 from U.S.
$92 million for the comparable period of 2012. EBIT margin was 28% for the three
months
ended June&nbsp;30, 2013. </FONT></P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-
family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">- 27 -

<P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New

<P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" 
ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Cost of net 
financial debt increased 21% to U.S.$47 million for the three months ended 
June&nbsp;30, 2013 from U.S.$39
million for the comparable period of 2012 due to the convertible bonds 
(&#147;OCEANE&#148;) issued in November 2012 and the vendor loan borrowed from 
Fugro. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><I>Income Taxes 
</I></B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" 
ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Income taxes 
increased to U.S.$35
million for the three months ended June&nbsp;30, 2013 from U.S.$27 million for 
the comparable period of 2012 mainly due to the increase of our income. Before 
deferred taxes on currency translation, the effective tax rate was 49% for the 
three months
ended June&nbsp;30, 2013 compared to 48% for the three months ended 
June&nbsp;30, 2012, both rates being impacted by foreign deemed taxation. 
</FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New

the three months ended June&nbsp;30, 2013 compared to a U.S.$34 million for the 
comparable period of 2012 as a result of the factors discussed above. 
</FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New

STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Operating revenues for our

million for the six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2013 from U.S.$849 million for 
the comparable period
of 2012, mainly due to the integration of Fugro&#146;s fleet as of 
February&nbsp;1, 2013. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; 
text-indent:4%" ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman"

intra-group sales, operating revenues increased 26% to U.S.$898 million for the
six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2013 from U.S.$712 million for the comparable 
period of 2012. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-
left:4%"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><I>Marine acquisition 
</I></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" 
ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Operating 
revenues from our Marine
acquisition business line for the six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2013 increased 
66% to U.S.$961 million from U.S.$580 million for the comparable period of 2012,
mainly due to the integration of Fugro&#146;s fleet as of February&nbsp;1, 2013,
which
is composed of four C-Class seismic vessels and two other seismic vessels <I>Geo
Barents</I> and <I>Geo Atlantic</I>, and good marine production. </FONT></P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-
family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><I>Land (and Airborne) acquisition 
</I></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" 
ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Operating 
revenues from our other acquisition businesses, including intra-group sales, 
decreased 11% to U.S.$238 million
for the six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2013, compared to U.S.$269 million for 
the six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2012. The winter campaign in North America 
was not as strong as last year and we operated in difficult safety conditions, 
notably in
North Africa. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-
left:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><U>Geology, 
Geophysics&nbsp;&amp; Reservoir </U></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" 
ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Operating 
revenues from our GGR segment for the six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2013 
increased 50% to U.S.$627 million from
U.S.$419 million for the comparable period of 2012 mainly due to strong 
performance in all businesses. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-
bottom:0px; margin-left:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" 
SIZE="2"><I>Multi-clients,
basin data and Data Management </I></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-
bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New 
Roman" SIZE="2">Multi-client and basin data revenues increased 69% to U.S.$338 
million for
the six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2013 from U.S.$200 million for the six months
ended June&nbsp;30, 2012 mainly due to the increase of prefunding revenues and 
higher after-sales. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" 
ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Prefunding 
revenues were U.S.$148 million for the six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2013 
compared to U.S.$88 million for the
six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2012, mainly focused in the Gulf of Mexico with 
the continuation of our IBALT program, offshore Angola, Australia and the North 
Sea. The cash prefunding rate was 64% for the six months ended June&nbsp;30, 
2013 compared
to 56% for the six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2012. </FONT></P> <P 
STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-
family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><I>Imaging&nbsp;&amp; Reservoir </I></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"
ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Operating 
revenues from our Imaging&nbsp;&amp; Reservoir business line increased 32% to 
U.S.$289 million for the six
months ended June&nbsp;30, 2013 from U.S.$219 million for the comparable period 
of 2012 in a buoyant market. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-
bottom:0px; margin-left:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" 
SIZE="2"><U>Equipment
</U></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" 
ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Operating 
revenues for our Equipment segment, including intra-group sales, decreased 20% 
to U.S.$505
million for the six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2013 from U.S.$633&nbsp;million 
for the comparable period of 2012. Internal sales represented 25% of total 
revenue for the six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2013. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" 
ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Excluding 
intra-group sales, operating revenues for our Equipment segment decreased 22% to
U.S.$378 million for the six
months ended June&nbsp;30, 2013 from U.S.$487 million for the comparable period 
of 2012. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-
indent:4%" ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" 
SIZE="2">This decrease was
mainly due to lower land equipment sales in the six months ended June&nbsp;30, 
2013 compared to the six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2012, when we had deliveries
of equipment for high-channel-count surveys in the Middle East. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New 
Roman" SIZE="2"><B><I>Operating Expenses </I></B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-
top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" ALIGN="justify"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Cost of operations, including 
depreciation and amortization, increased 13% to U.S.$1,470 million for the six 
months ended June&nbsp;30, 2013 from U.S.$1,303 million for the comparable 
period of 2012,
mainly due to the integration of Fugro&#146;s Geoscience Division. The multi-
client amortization expenses correspond to 56% of multi-client revenues for the 
six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2013 compared to 72% for the comparable period of
2012. As a
percentage of operating revenues, cost of operations decreased to 77% for the 
six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2013 from 81% for the comparable period of 2012. 
Gross profit increased 37% to U.S.$434 million for the six months ended 
June&nbsp;30, 2013
from U.S.$316 million for the comparable period of 2012, representing 23% and 
20% of operating revenues, respectively. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-
top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" ALIGN="justify"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Research and development 
expenditures increased 15% to U.S.$51 million for the six months ended 
June&nbsp;30, 2013, from U.S.$45 million for the comparable period of 2012, 
representing 3% of operating
revenues for both periods. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-
bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New 
Roman" SIZE="2">Marketing and selling expenses increased 35% to U.S.$63 million 
for the six months
ended June&nbsp;30, 2013 from U.S.$47 million for the comparable period of 2012.
</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" 
ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">General and 
administrative
expenses increased 14% to U.S.$105 million for the six months ended 
June&nbsp;30, 2013 from U.S.$92 million for the comparable period of 2012. As a 
percentage of operating revenues, general and administrative expenses 
represented 6% for both
periods. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-
indent:4%" ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" 
SIZE="2">Other revenues amounted to U.S.$58 million for the six months ended 
June&nbsp;30, 2013, mainly due
to (i)&nbsp;U.S.$20 million gain on the sale of our remaining 10% stake in
Spectrum ASA, (ii)&nbsp;U.S.$85 million gain related to the contribution of 
shallow-water and OBC assets to our Seabed joint-venture with Fugro, 
(iii)&nbsp;U.S.$17 million of
Fugro Geoscience Division acquisition costs, and (iv)&nbsp;U.S.$23 million of 
provisions for restructuring costs related to acquired vessels. Other revenues 
of U.S.$6 million for the six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2012 were mainly 
related to the
contribution of the seismic vessel <I>Amadeus</I> to our Vietnamese joint-
venture. </FONT></P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New 
Roman" SIZE="2"><B><I>Equity in Income of Affiliates </I></B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" 
ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Income from 
investments accounted for under the equity method decreased to U.S.$6 million 
for the six months ended
June&nbsp;30, 2013 from U.S.$14 million for the comparable period of 2012, 
mainly due to the slow start of our Seabed joint-venture with Fugro. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New 
Roman" SIZE="2"><B><I>Earnings before interest and tax (&#147;EBIT&#148;) 
</I></B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" 
ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">EBIT, as 
disclosed in note 6 to our Consolidated Financial Statements, amounted to U.S.
$279 million for the six months
ended June&nbsp;30, 2013 compared to U.S.$153 million for the six months ended 
June&nbsp;30, 2012 as a result of the factors described above. </FONT></P> <P 
STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" ALIGN="justify"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">EBIT from our Acquisition segment 
were U.S.$75 million for the six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2013 compared to a 
U.S.$34 million loss for the six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2012. EBIT margin 
was 6% for
the six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2013. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-
top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-
family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">EBIT from our GGR segment were U.S.$177 million
for the six months
ended June&nbsp;30, 2013 compared to U.S.$67 million for the six months ended 
June&nbsp;30, 2012. EBIT margin was 28% for the six months ended June&nbsp;30, 
2013. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" 
ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">EBIT from our
Equipment segment were U.S.$140 million for six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2013 
from U.S.$207 million for
the comparable period of 2012. EBIT margin was 28% for the six months ended 
June&nbsp;30, 2013. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-
bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><I>Financial 
Income and Expenses
</I></B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" 
ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Cost of net 
financial debt increased 20% to U.S.$93 million for the six months ended 
June&nbsp;30,
2013 from U.S.$77 million for the comparable period of 2012 due to the 
convertible bonds (&#147;OCEANE&#148;) issued in November 2012 and the vendor 
loan borrowed from Fugro. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"
ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Other 
financial expenses amounted to U.S.$5 million for the six months ended 
June&nbsp;30, 2013 compared to a gain of
U.S.$1 million for comparable period of 2012, mainly due to currency 
fluctuations. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT 
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><I>Income Taxes 
</I></B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" 
ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Income taxes 
increased to U.S.$67 million for the six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2013 from 
U.S.$46 million for the
comparable period of 2012 mainly due to the increase of our income. Before 
deferred taxes on currency translation, the effective tax rate was 35% for the 
six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2013. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-
top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><I>Net Income 
</I></B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" 
ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Net income 
was U.S.$115 million for the
six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2013 compared to a U.S.$31 million for the 
comparable period of 2012 as a result of the factors discussed above. 
</FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New 
Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Liquidity and Capital Resources </B></FONT></P> <P 
STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" ALIGN="justify"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Our principal capital needs are for
the funding of ongoing operations, capital expenditures (particularly repairs 
and improvements to our seismic vessels), investments in our multi-client data 
library and
acquisitions. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-
indent:4%" ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">We
intend to fund ongoing operations and debt service requirements through cash 
generated by
operations. Our ability to make scheduled payments of principal, or to pay the 
interest or additional amounts, if any, on, or to refinance our indebtedness, or
to fund planned capital expenditures will depend on our future performance, 
which, to a
certain extent, is subject to general economic, financial, competitive, 
legislative, regulatory and other factors that are beyond our control. Based 
upon the current level of operations and our near-to mid-term debt repayment 
schedule, we believe
that cash flow from operations, available cash and cash equivalents, together 
with liquidity available under our new U.S.$165 million U.S. revolving facility 
and our new U.S.$325 million French revolving facility will be adequate to meet 
our
liquidity needs for the next twelve months. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-
top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" 
SIZE="2"><B>Cash Flows </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-
bottom:0px"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><I>Operations 
</I></B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" 
ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Net cash 
provided by operating
activities was U.S.$267 million for the six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2013 
compared to U.S.$296 million for the comparable period of 2012. Before changes 
in working capital, net cash provided by operating activities for the six months
ended
June&nbsp;30, 2013 was U.S.$497 million compared to U.S.$361 million for the 
comparable period for 2012. Changes in working capital had a negative impact on 
cash from operating activities of U.S.$230 million in the six months ended 
June&nbsp;30,
2013 </FONT></P>

STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-

<P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New

STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Net cash used in investing 
activities was U.S.$1,294 million in the six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2013 
compared to U.S.$410 million for the six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2012. 
</FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" 
ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">On

million (including U.S.$9 million cash contributed to our Seabed joint-venture),
net of U.S.$24 million of cash acquired, for Fugro&#146;s Geoscience Division,

be

with a net investment of U.S.$53 million, after an initial payment of U.S.$50 
million and an additional payment of U.S.$3 million in April 2012. </FONT></P> 
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"

related to marine equipment with notably the purchase of RD sentinel streamers. 
During the six
months ended June&nbsp;30, 2012, our capital expenditures amounted to U.S.$213 
million and were mainly related to the upgrade of the seismic vessel <I>Oceanic 
Champion</I> and the purchases of land equipment. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" 
ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">During the 
six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2013, we invested U.S.$235 million in multi-
client data, primarily offshore
Angola and Gulf of Mexico, and onshore U.S., compared to U.S.$157 million for 
the six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2012. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-
top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" ALIGN="justify"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">As of June&nbsp;30, 2013, the net 
book value of our multi-client data library was U.S.$751 million compared to 
U.S$604 million as of December&nbsp;31, 2012. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New 
Roman" SIZE="2"><B><I>Financing activities </I></B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-

STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Net cash used in financing 
activities during the six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2013 was U.S.$150 million 
compared to net cash used of U.S.$94 million for the six months ended 
June&nbsp;30, 2012.
</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" 
ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">During the 
six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2013, &#128;85&nbsp;million from our French 
revolving facility were
drawn and fully repaid. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-
bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Net Financial 
debt </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"
ALIGN="justify"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Net financial debt as of 
June&nbsp;30, 2013 was U.S.$2,170 million compared to U.S.$785 million as of 
December&nbsp;31, 2012. The ratio of net financial debt to equity was 47% as of 
June&nbsp;30, 2013
compared to 17% as of December&nbsp;31, 2012 (or 36% as of December&nbsp;31, 
2012 excluding the impact of the financing of the Fugro transaction). 
</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" 
ALIGN="justify"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">&#147;Gross financial debt&#148; is
defined as the amount of bank overdrafts, plus current portion of financial 
debt, plus financial debt, and &#147;net financial debt&#148; is defined as 
gross financial
debt less cash and cash equivalents. Net financial debt is presented as 
additional information because we understand that certain investors believe that
netting cash against debt provides a clearer picture of the financial liability 
exposure.
However, other companies may present net financial debt differently than we do. 
Net financial debt is not a measure of financial performance under IFRS and 
should not be considered as an alternative to any other measures of performance 
derived in
accordance with IFRS. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px;

<h5 align="left"><a href="#toc">Table of Contents</a></h5>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New 
Roman" SIZE="2"><B>EBIT and EBITDAS </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" 
ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">We define 
EBIT as operating income plus our share of income in companies accounted for 
under the equity method. EBIT is
presented as additional information because our management uses it to capture 
the contribution to our results of the significant businesses that we manage 
through our joint ventures. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" 
ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">We define 
EBITDAS as earnings before interest, tax, depreciation, amortization net of 
amortization costs capitalized to
multi-client surveys, and share-based compensation cost. Share-based 
compensation includes both stock options and shares issued under our performance
share allocation plans. EBITDAS is presented as additional information because 
we understand that
it is a measure used by certain investors to determine our operating cash flow 
and historical ability to meet debt service and capital expenditure 
requirements. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" 
ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">However, 
other companies may present EBIT and EBITDAS and related measures differently 
than we do. EBIT and EBITDAS are
not measures of financial performance under IFRS and should not be considered as
an alternative to cash flow from operating activities or as a measure of 
liquidity or an alternative to net income as indicators of our operating 
performance or any
other measures of performance derived in accordance with IFRS. </FONT></P> <P 
STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" ALIGN="justify"><FONT 
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">EBIT for the six months ended 
June&nbsp;30,
2013 was U.S.$279 million compared to U.S.$153 million for the comparable period
of 2012, representing 15% and 9% of operating revenues, respectively. 
</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" 
ALIGN="justify"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The following table presents a 
reconciliation of EBIT to &#147;operating income&#148; for the periods 
indicated: </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-
bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
