<P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New 
Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Reconciliation of EBITDAS to U.S. GAAP </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New 
Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Summary of differences between IFRS and U.S. GAAP with 
respect to EBITDAS </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px" 
ALIGN="justify"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The principal differences between 
IFRS and U.S. GAAP as they relate to our EBITDAS relate to the treatment of 
pension plans and development costs. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-
top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><I>Pension plan 
</I></B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" 
ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Under IFRS, 
in accordance with IAS 19
&#150; Revised, actuarial gains or losses are recognized in the statement of 
recognized income and expense (SORIE) attributable to shareholders. </FONT></P> 
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" 
ALIGN="justify"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Under U.S. GAAP, we apply Statement
158 &#147;Employers&#146; Accounting for Defined Benefit Pension and Other 
Postretirement Plan, an amendment of FASB Statements No.&nbsp;87, 88, 106, and 
132(R)&#148;,
effective for fiscal years ending after December&nbsp;15, 2006. </FONT></P> <P 
STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" ALIGN="justify"><FONT 
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Gains or losses are amortized over 
the
remaining service period of employees expected to receive benefits under the 
plan, and therefore recognized in the income statement. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New 
Roman" SIZE="2"><B><I>Development costs </I></B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-
family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Under IFRS, expenditure on development 
activities, whereby research findings are applied to a plan or design for the 
production of new or
substantially improved products and processes, is capitalized if: </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" 
CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New 
Roman" SIZE="2">&#149;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times
New Roman" SIZE="2">the project is clearly defined, and costs are separately 
identified and reliably measured, </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" 
CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New 
Roman" SIZE="2">&#149;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times
New Roman" SIZE="2">the product or process is technically and commercially 
feasible, </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" 
CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New 
Roman" SIZE="2">&#149;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times
New Roman" SIZE="2">the Group has sufficient resources to complete development, 
and </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" 
CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New 
Roman" SIZE="2">&#149;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times
New Roman" SIZE="2">The intangible asset is likely to generate future economic 
benefits. </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-
family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Under U.S. GAAP, all expenditures related to 
research and development are recognized as an expense in the income statement. 
</FONT></P>
